    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nCloudflare\nBlogger\ncoreBos\nCraftQL\nElementor\nGhost\nMedium\nNetlify\nSimvoly\nSquarespace\nTilda\nUnbounce\nWebflow\nWix\nWordPress\nWordPress (legacy)\nWP All Import\nWP Webhooks\nYoast\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsWebsite BuildingCloudflare\nCloudflare\n\nThe Cloudflare modules enable you to monitor, create, or update zones and monitor, create, list, patch, delete, or export/import DNS records in your Cloudflare account.\n\nGetting Started with Cloudflare\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Cloudflare account\n\nIn order to use Cloudflare with Make, it is necessary to have a Cloudflare account. If you do not have one, you can create a Cloudflare account at dash.cloudflare.com/sign-up.\n\nConnecting Cloudflare to Make\n\nTo connect your Cloudflare account to Make, you'll need to create an API token or retrieve an API Key in your Cloudflare account.\n\nChoose one of the options for establishing a connection:\n\nAPI Token (allows scoped and permissioned access to resources, and uses the RFC compliant Authorization Bearer Token Header)\n\nAPI Key\n\nConnecting Using an API Token\n\n1. Log in to your Cloudflare account.\n\n2. Click your profile icon in the top-right corner, and select the My Profile option.\n\n3. Open the API Tokens tab, and click the Create Token button.\n\n4. On the API Tokens page, click the Get Started button to create a custom token.\n\n5. Enter the desired name for your token, and add required permissions and additional permissions needed for the modules you want to use in your scenario. Then click Continue to summary and Create a Token.\n\nREQUIRED PERMISSIONS\n\n\t\n\nAccount:Account Settings:Read\n\nUser:User Details:Read\n\nZone:Zone:Read\n\nAdditional Permissions\n\nMODULE NAME\n\n\t\n\nPERMISSION REQUIRED FOR THE MODULE\n\n\n\n\nWatch Zones\n\n\t\n\nZone:Zone:Read\n\n\n\n\nCreate a Zone\n\n\t\n\nZone:Zone:Edit\n\n\n\n\nChange a Zone's SSL Setting\n\n\t\n\nZone:Zone Settings:Edit\n\n\n\n\nChange a Zone's Security Level\n\n\t\n\nZone:Zone Settings:Edit\n\n\n\n\nTurn a Zone into Development Mode\n\n\t\n\nZone:Zone Settings:Edit\n\n\n\n\nWatch DNS Records\n\n\t\n\nZone:DNS:Read\n\n\n\n\nCreate a DNS Record\n\n\t\n\nZone:DNS:Edit\n\n\n\n\nList DNS Records\n\n\t\n\nZone:DNS:Read\n\n\n\n\nPatch a DNS Record\n\n\t\n\nZone:DNS:Edit\n\n\n\n\nDelete a DNS Record\n\n\t\n\nZone:DNS:Edit\n\n\n\n\nExport DNS Records\n\n\t\n\nZone:DNS:Read\n\n\n\n\nImport DNS Records\n\n\t\n\nZone:DNS:Edit\n\n\n\n\nCreate a Certificate\n\n\t\n\nRequires the API Key authentication.\n\n\n\n\nList Certificates\n\n\t\n\nRequires the API Key authentication.\n\n\n\n\nRevoke a Certificate\n\n\t\n\nRequires the API Key authentication.\n\n\n\n\nWatch User Billings\n\n\t\n\nRequires the API Key authentication.\n\n6. Copy the token provided.\n\n7. Go to Make, open the Cloudflare module's Create a connection dialog, and select the API Token option in the Authentication Method field.\n\n8. Enter the API Token you have copied in step 6 to the respective field, and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nThe connection has been established. You can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nConnecting Using API Key\n\n1. Log in to your Cloudflare account.\n\n2. Click your profile icon in the top-right corner, and select the My Profile option.\n\n3. Open the API Tokens tab, and click the View button for the Global API Key. Enter the password, and copy the displayed Global API Key.\n\n4. Go to Make, open the Cloudflare module's Create a connection dialog, and select the API Key option in the Authentication Method field.\n\n5. Enter the Global API Key you have copied in step 3 to the respective field, enter your account email, and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nThe connection has been established. You can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nZones\n\nA Zone is a domain name along with its subdomains and other identities.\n\nWatch Zones\n\nRetrieves details when a zone is created, updated, or activated.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nEvent\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to watch created, modified, or activated zones\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of zones Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nCreate a Zone\n\nCreates a new zone.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nDomain Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the domain name of the site you want to add.\n\n\n\n\nAccount ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter or select the account ID.\n\nIf the account ID is not provided in the drop-down menu, you can obtain the account ID in the URL of your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nSkip fetching current DNS records\n\n\t\n\nEnable this option to skip automatic attempt to fetch existing DNS records.\n\n\n\n\nType\n\n\t\n\nSelect the type. A full zone implies that DNS is hosted with Cloudflare. A partial zone is typically a partner-hosted zone or a CNAME setup.\n\nChange a Zone's SSL Setting\n\nChanges the SSL setting of the specified site.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to change the SSL setting for.\n\n\n\n\nSSL Setting\n\n\t\n\nOff (Not Secure) No SSL between the visitor and Cloudflare, and no SSL between Cloudflare and your web server (all HTTP traffic).\n\nFlexible SSL between the visitor and Cloudflare. The visitor sees HTTPS on your site, but no SSL between Cloudflare and your web server. You don't need to have an SSL certificate on your web server, but your visitors will still see the site as being HTTPS enabled.\n\nFull SSL between the visitor and Cloudflare. The visitor sees HTTPS on your site and SSL between Cloudflare and your web server. You'll need to have your own SSL certificate or self-signed certificate, at the very least.\n\nFull (strict) SSL between the visitor and Cloudflare. The visitor sees HTTPS on your site and SSL between Cloudflare and your web server. You'll need to have a valid SSL certificate installed on your web server. This certificate must be signed by a certificate authority, have an expiration date in the future, and respond for the request domain name (hostname).\n\nChange a Zone's Security Level\n\nAdjusts the security settings.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to change the security level for.\n\n\n\n\nSecurity Level\n\n\t\n\nSelect the security level you want to set for the zone specified above.\n\nEssentially off Only challenges IP addresses with the worst reputation.\n\nLow Challenges only the most threatening visitors.\n\nMedium Challenges both moderate threat visitors and the most threatening visitors.\n\nHigh Challenges all visitors that exhibit threatening behavior within the last 14 days.\n\nI’m Under Attack! Only for use if your website is currently under a DDoS attack.\n\nTurn a Zone into Development Mode\n\nModifies the development mode setting of the zone.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to enable the development mode for.\n\n\n\n\nDevelopment mode\n\n\t\n\nEnable this option to turn on the development mode.\n\nDNS Records\nWatch DNS Records\n\nReturns DNS record details when a DNS record is created or modified.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to watch for DNS records.\n\n\n\n\nEvent\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to watch created or modified DNS records.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of DNS records Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nCreate a DNS Record\n\nCreates a new DNS record for a zone.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to create a new DNS record for.\n\n\n\n\nType\n\n\t\n\nSelect the type of the new DNS record. See the Cloudflare documentation for each type's fields.\n\nList DNS Records\n\nReturns DNS records based on specified criteria.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to list DNS records for.\n\n\n\n\nRequirement\n\n\t\n\nSelect the logical operator. Indicate whether to match all search requirements or at least one (any).\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the DNS record name to filter results by.\n\n\n\n\nContent\n\n\t\n\nEnter the content of the DNS record to filter results by.\n\n\n\n\nType\n\n\t\n\nSelect the type of the DNS record to filter results by.\n\n\n\n\nProxied\n\n\t\n\nDNS record proxied status.\n\n\n\n\nOrder\n\n\t\n\nSelect the order in which you want to sort returned DNS records.\n\n\n\n\nDirection\n\n\t\n\nSelect the order of the returned domains.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of DNS records Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nPatch a DNS Record\n\nPartially updates a DNS record.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to update a DNS record for.\n\n\n\n\nDNS Record ID\n\n\t\n\nMap or select the identifier of the DNS record you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nType\n\n\t\n\nSelect the type of DNS record.\n\nDelete a DNS Record\n\nRemoves a DNS record.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to delete a DNS record from.\n\n\n\n\nDNS Record ID\n\n\t\n\nMap or select the identifier of the DNS record you want to delete.\n\nExport DNS Records\n\nDownloads a BIND configuration file.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to download a BIND configuration file for.\n\n\n\n\nFile Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the file name without .zone extension. Leave this field blank to use {zone_name}_{current_datetime}.zone as the file name.\n\nImport DNS Records\n\nUploads a BIND configuration file.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to upload a BIND configuration file to.\n\n\n\n\nSource File\n\n\t\n\nMap the file you want to upload from the previous module (e.g. HTTP > Get a File or Google Drive > Download a File), or enter the file name and file data manually.\n\nOrigin CA\nCreate a Certificate\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nHostnames\n\n\t\n\nAdd hostnames you want to bind to the certificate.\n\n\n\n\nRequested Validity\n\n\t\n\nSelect the number of days for which the certificate should be valid.\n\n\n\n\nRequest Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect the signature type desired on the certificate.\n\n\n\n\nCertificate Signing Request\n\n\t\n\nEnter the CSR (a block of encoded text).\n\nList Certificates\n\nRetrieves origin certificates for the specified zone.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to list certificates from.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of certificates Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nRevoke a Certificate\n\nRevoke an existing Origin CA certificate.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nZone ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the zone ID, or select the zone you want to revoke a certificate from.\n\n\n\n\nCertificate ID\n\n\t\n\nMap the Certificate ID of the certificate you want to revoke.\n\nBillings\nWatch User Billings\n\nRetrieves billing history details when the authorized user is billed.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of billing histories Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nAllows you to perform a custom API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Cloudflare account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.cloudflare.com/client. For example: /v4/user.\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Cloudflare API v4 Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGETto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOSTto create a new entry.\n\nPUTto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCHto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETEto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we've already done this for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Zones\n\nThe following API call returns all zones in your Cloudflare account:\n\nURL:/v4/zones\n\nMethod:GET\n\nThe result can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > result. In our example, 2 zones were returned:\n\nCommon Problems\nThe operation failed with an error. [403] Error 9109: Unauthorized to access requested resource\n\nAdd the permission to your API Token that is required by the module you want to use. Please see the additional permissions list.\n\nThe operation failed with an error. [501] Error 10000: API Tokens are not supported by this API for now.\n\nConnect using an API Key.\n\nCloudflare\nGetting Started with Cloudflare\nConnecting Cloudflare to Make\nConnecting Using an API Token\nAdditional Permissions\nConnecting Using API Key\nZones\nWatch Zones\nCreate a Zone\nChange a Zone's SSL Setting\nChange a Zone's Security Level\nTurn a Zone into Development Mode\nDNS Records\nWatch DNS Records\nCreate a DNS Record\nList DNS Records\nPatch a DNS Record\nDelete a DNS Record\nExport DNS Records\nImport DNS Records\nOrigin CA\nCreate a Certificate\nList Certificates\nRevoke a Certificate\nBillings\nWatch User Billings\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Zones\nCommon Problems\nThe operation failed with an error. The minimum value is 3 (least magnification). The maximum value is 17 (most magnification).\n\n\n\n\nNavigate to Location\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Yes option to navigate to the location right after opening the app.\n\nSearch an Address\n\nCreates a link to search for an address.\n\nQuery\n\n\t\n\nEnter the latitude of the map's center point.\n\nNavigate to a Favorite\n\nCreates a link to navigate to your favorite location.\n\nName of the favorite location\n\n\t\n\nName of the favorite location that you have stored in your Waze app, e.g. work, or home.\n\n\n\n\nNavigate to Location\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Yes option to navigate to the location right after opening the app.\n\nWaze Deep Links\nGetting Started with Waze Deep Links\nActions\nGenerate URL for a Pin\nNavigate to a Location\nSearch an Address\nNavigate to a Favorite\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

    "title": "Sendcloud",
    "url": "https://www.make.com/en/help/apps/travel/sendcloud#content-wrapper",
    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nDetrack\nFoursquare\nGoogle Maps\nGPS Tools\nMyCarTracks\nOpenWeatherMap\nSendcloud\nSendle\nWaze Deep Links\nWeather\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsTravelSendcloud\nSendcloud\n\nThe Sendcloud modules allow you to watch, create, list, retrieve, and delete the parcel, returns, invoices, brands, and integrations in your Sendcloud account.\n\nGetting Started with Sendcloud\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Sendcloud account\n\nIn order to use Sendcloud with Make, it is necessary to have a Sendcloud account. If you do not have one, you can create a Sendcloud account at sendcloud.com.\n\nConnecting Sendcloud to Make\n\nTo connect your Sendcloud account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Sendcloud account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\n1. Log in to your Sendcloud account.\n\n2. Click Settings () > Integrations > Sendcloud API.\n\n3. Enter a name for the API and click Save.\n\n4. Copy the Public Key and Secret Key details to a safe place and Click Save.\n\n5. Go to Make and open the Sendcloud module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n6. In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\n7. In the Public Key and Secret Key fields, enter the details copied in step 4 respectively, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nParcel\nWatch Parcel Status\n\nTriggers when a parcel status is changed.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Sendcloud account.\n\nSee Connecting to Sendcloud Webhook using Make to add the webhook to your Sendcloud account.\n\nList Parcels\n\nReturns a list of parcels.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nParcel Status\n\n\t\n\nSelect the parcel status whose details you want to list. For example, delivered.\n\n\n\n\nTracking Number\n\n\t\n\nSelect the parcel tracking number to list the parcels with the specified number.\n\n\n\n\nOrder Number\n\n\t\n\nSelect the parcel's order number whose details you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nAnnounced After\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date to list all the parcels announced after the specified date. See the list of supported formats.\n\n\n\n\nUpdated After\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date to list all the parcels updated after the specified date. See the list of supported formats.\n\n\n\n\nParcel IDs\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Parcel IDs whose details you want to list.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of parcels Make should return during one scenario execution cycle.\n\nGet a Parcel\n\nReturns a specified parcel.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nParcel ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Parcel ID whose details you want to retrieve.\n\nCreate a Parcel\n\nCreates a new parcel.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's name.\n\n\n\n\nAddress\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's address.\n\n\n\n\nHouse Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's house number.\n\n\n\n\nCity\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's city name.\n\n\n\n\nPostal Code\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's area postal code.\n\n\n\n\nCountry\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's country name.\n\n\n\n\nCompany Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's company name to which the parcel will be shipped to.\n\n\n\n\nAdditional Address\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's alternative address.\n\n\n\n\nCountry State\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's two-character state code. For example, NY for New York.\n\n\n\n\nTelephone\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's phone number.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's email address.\n\n\n\n\nSender Address\n\n\t\n\nEnter the sender's address who is sending the parcel.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Invoice Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the parcel's invoice number if it is shipped outside the EU region.\n\n\n\n\nCustom Shipment Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect the parcel type:\n\nGift\n\nDocuments\n\nCommercial Address\n\nReturned Goods\n\n\n\n\nExternal Reference\n\n\t\n\nEnter the unique external reference number with which you can identify a parcel.\n\n\n\n\nRequest Label\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether a label is requested for the parcel.\n\n\n\n\nRequest Label Async\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether a label is requested asynchronously for the parcel.\n\n\n\n\nTo Service Point\n\n\t\n\nEnter the parcel's Service Point ID.\n\n\n\n\nInsured Value\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Sendcloud Insurance amount to add to the parcel. The entered value must be a multiple of 100 and maxes out at 2500 or 5000 depending on the carrier. This field does not take the carrier/shipping method insurance into consideration\n\n\n\n\nTotal Insured Value\n\n\t\n\nEnter the parcel's total insurance amount. The entered value must be a multiple of 100 and maxes out at 2500 or 5000 depending on the carrier.\n\nThis field automatically calculates the Sendcloud Insurance you need to add and your shipping method's insurance so it matches the exact value you have given. As an example, DPD insures all their shipments by 520€ by default. If you pass the total insured value, 5000, then your shipment will have total insurance coverage of 5000€, but you are only paying for 4480€.\n\n\n\n\nOrder Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the parcel order number.\n\n\n\n\nIntegration ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the integration option for the parcel. You must create integrations in your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nShipment UUID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the unique identifier assigned to the shipment with the Sendcloud system.\n\n\n\n\nParcel Items\n\n\t\n\nAdd the parcel items:\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's details.\n\n\n\n\nQuantity\n\n\t\n\nEnter the number of items.\n\n\n\n\nWeight\n\n\t\n\nEnter the single item weight in kilograms.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nEnter the single item price.\n\n\n\n\nHarmonized System Code\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's Harmonized System Code.\n\n\n\n\nOrigin Country\n\n\t\n\nEnter the two-character country code if the parcel is shipped outside the EU region.\n\n\n\n\nSKU\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's stock-keeping unit number.\n\n\n\n\nProduct ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's Product ID.\n\n\n\n\nKey\n\n\t\n\nEnter custom key details for the item.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nEnter the key value.\n\n\n\n\nWeight\n\n\t\n\nEnter the weight of the parcel in kilograms. If no weight is specified, the default weight in settings is used.\n\n\n\n\nIs Return\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the item is returnable.\n\n\n\n\nTotal Order Value\n\n\t\n\nEnter the amount paid by the buyer through various payment methods. For example, 99.9.\n\nUpdate a Parcel\n\nUpdates a parcel with the option to request a label - it hasn't been requested before.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nParcel ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Parcel ID whose details you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's name.\n\n\n\n\nAddress\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's address.\n\n\n\n\nHouse Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's house number.\n\n\n\n\nCity\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's city name.\n\n\n\n\nPostal Code\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's area postal code.\n\n\n\n\nCountry\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's country name.\n\n\n\n\nCompany Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's company name to which the parcel will be shipped to.\n\n\n\n\nAdditional Address\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's alternative address.\n\n\n\n\nCountry State\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's two-character state code. This field does not take the carrier/shipping method insurance into consideration\n\n\n\n\nTotal Insured Value\n\n\t\n\nEnter the parcel's total insurance amount. The entered value must be a multiple of 100 and max out at 2500 or 5000 depending on the carrier.\n\nThis field automatically calculates the Sendcloud Insurance you need to add and your shipping method's insurance so it matches the exact value you have given. As an example, DPD ensures all their shipments by 520€ by default. If you pass the total insured value, 5000, then your shipment will have total insurance coverage of 5000€, but you are only paying for 4480€.\n\n\n\n\nOrder Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the parcel order number.\n\n\n\n\nIntegration ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the integration option for the parcel. You must create integrations in your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nParcel Items\n\n\t\n\nAdd the parcel items:\n\nDescription\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's details.\n\n\n\n\nQuantity\n\n\t\n\nEnter the number of items.\n\n\n\n\nWeight\n\n\t\n\nEnter the single item weight in kilograms.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nEnter the single item price.\n\n\n\n\nHarmonized System Code\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's Harmonized System Code.\n\n\n\n\nOrigin Country\n\n\t\n\nEnter the two-character country code if the parcel is shipped outside of the EU region.\n\n\n\n\nSKU\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's stock-keeping unit number.\n\n\n\n\nProduct ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the item's Product ID.\n\n\n\n\nKey\n\n\t\n\nEnter custom key details for the item.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nEnter the key value.\n\n\n\n\nWeight\n\n\t\n\nEnter the weight of the parcel in kilograms. For example, 99.9.\n\nDownload Parcel Document\n\nDownloads a parcel document.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nMapping\n\n\t\n\nSelect the option to choose the parcel document you want to download:\n\nMap\n\nChoose from List\n\n\n\n\nParcel ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Parcel ID whose documents you want to download.\n\n\n\n\nDocument Type\n\n\t\n\nSelect the document type you want to download.\n\n\n\n\nFormat\n\n\t\n\nSelect the format in which you want to download the document:\n\nPDF\n\nZPL\n\nPNG\n\nCancels a Parcel\n\nCancels or deletes a parcel depending on its status and other parameters.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Sendcloud account.\n\n\n\n\nParcel ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Parcel ID you want to delete. point.\n\n\n\n\nIs Return\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the shipping method you want to list includes a return policy.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of shipping methods Make should return If you do not have one, you can create a MyCarTracks account at mycartracks.com.\n\nConnecting MyCarTracks to Make\n\nTo connect your MyCarTracks account to Make you need to obtain the Client ID and Client Secret from your MyCarTracks account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\n1. Log in to your MyCarTracks account.\n\n2. Click Your Profile Icon > Settings > API > Generate.\n\n3. Copy the Client ID and Client Secret details to a safe place.\n\n4. Go to Make and open the MyCarTrack module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n5. In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\n6. If you do not have an OpenWeatherMap account yet, you can create one at OpenWeatherMap.org.\n\nConnecting OpenWeatherMap to Make\n\nTo connect your OpenWeatherMap account to Make, follow the general instructions for Connecting to services. Clicking the Continue button will open a form for entering your OpenWeatherMap API key. You will find the API key after logging into your OpenWeatherMap account under Settings.\n\nOnce you have entered the API key and saved the form, you can continue creating your scenario. OpenWeatherMap may take up to 60 minutes to activate the newly generated API key. Your integration may therefore not work immediately after being created. More information can be found here.\n\nActions\nGet current weather\n\nThis module retrieves current weather information including coordinates, temperature, atmospheric pressure, air humidity, wind speed and direction, sunrise time, sunset time, word description (e.g. \"clear sky\").\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your OpenWeatherMap account.\n\n\n\n\nI want to enter a location by\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to define city name or coordinates (using longitude and latitude)\n\n\n\n\nCity\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired city name and country code divided by a comma, use two-letter ISO 3166 country codes (e.g. Granada, ES)\n\nGet daily weather forecast\n\nThis module allows you to retrieve the 15 day daily weather forecast for the specified location.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your OpenWeatherMap account.\n\n\n\n\nDays\n\n\t\n\nSelect the days you want to know the forecast for.\n\n\n\n\nI want to enter a location by\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to define city name or coordinates (using longitude and latitude)\n\n\n\n\nCity\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired city name and country code divided by a comma, use two-letter ISO 3166 country codes (e.g. Granada, ES)\n\nOpenWeatherMap\nGetting Started with OpenWeatherMap\nPrerequisites\nConnecting OpenWeatherMap to Make\nActions\nGet current weather\nGet daily weather forecast\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nDetrack\nFoursquare\nGoogle Maps\nGPS Tools\nMyCarTracks\nOpenWeatherMap\nSendcloud\nSendle\nWaze Deep Links\nWeather\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsTravelGPS Tools\nGPS Tools\n\nThe GPS Tools modules enable you to calculate and sort distances based on geographical coordinates.\n\nGetting Started with GPS Tools\n\nPrerequisites\n\nGPS coordinates (latitude and longitude) of the desired locations\n\nCalculate and Sort Distance\nCalculate Distance\n\nCalculates the direct distance between two geographical coordinates.\n\nOrigin Latitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the latitude of the first location in the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. 41.40338\n\n\n\n\nOrigin Longitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the longitude of the first location in the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. 2.17403\n\n\n\n\nDestination Latitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the latitude of the second location in the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. 16.822043\n\n\n\n\nDestination Longitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the longitude of the second location. In the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. -93.079391\n\nFind the Closest Destination\n\nCalculates the direct distance to multiple destinations and returns the closest one.\n\nOrigin Latitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the latitude of the first location in the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. 41.40338\n\n\n\n\nOrigin Longitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the longitude of the first location in the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. 2.17403\n\n\n\n\nDestination\n\n\t\n\nSpecify the locations (by latitude and longitude in decimal degrees) from which you want to find the closest one.\n\nSort Distance\n\nCalculates the direct distance to multiple destinations and sorts them by the distance.\n\nOrigin Latitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the latitude of the first location in the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. 41.40338\n\n\n\n\nOrigin Longitude\n\n\t\n\nEnter the longitude of the first location in the following format:\n\nDecimal degrees, e.g. 2.17403\n\n\n\n\nSort Order\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to return destinations in ascending or descending order.\n\n\n\n\nReturn Limit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of destinations Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\n\n\n\nDestination\n\n\t\n\nSpecify the locations (by latitude and longitude in decimal degrees) which you want to sort by distance.\n\nGPS Tools\nGetting Started with GPS Tools\nCalculate and Sort Distance\nCalculate Distance\nFind the Closest Destination\nSort Distance\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can create an account at detrack.com.\n\nRefer to the Detrack API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Detrack to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Detrack.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Detrack\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Detrack account:\n\nLog in to your Detrack account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click Integrations > API Key.\n\nClick Generate New Key.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Detrack in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Detrack module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Detrack modules.     "url": "https://www.make.com/en/help/apps/surveys-and-forms/jotform#content-wrapper",
    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\n123FormBuilder\nAidaForm\nBasin\nCognito Forms\nContact Form 7\nFastField\nFormCrafts\nFormidable Forms\nFormsite\nGoogle Forms\nGravity Forms\nInMoment\nJotform\nPaperform\nPointerpro\nPoptin\nQuestionPro\nRefiner\nResponseSuite\nSoundCloud\nSurvey123\nSurveybot\nSurveyMonkey\nSurveySparrow\nTally\nTypebot\nTypeform\nVideoAsk\nWufoo\nZoho Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsSurveys and FormsJotform\nJotform\n\nWith Jotform modules in Make, you can manage the forms and submissions in your Jotform account.\n\nTo use the Jotform modules, you must have a Jotform account. You can create an account at jotform.com.\n\nRefer to the Jotform API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Jotform to Make\n\nTo connect your Jotform account to Make, you must first obtain the API Key from your Jotform account. Refer to the Daily API Call Limits guide for information regarding API Key request limitations.\n\nLog in to your Jotform account.\n\nIn the top-right corner, click on your profile icon > Settings.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click on the API tab.\n\nClick on the Create New Key button.\n\nNext to the API Key value, click within the Permissions box and select the API Key's access level. To use Jotform modules that write data into your Jotform account, for example Create a New Form and Add Questions to Form, select Full Access.\n\nCopy the API Key value shown. You will use this key in the API Key field in Make.\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Jotform module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied in Step 6.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your Enterprise Domain to connect to your enterprise address or select whether your Jotform account is in HIPAA Safe Mode to redirect to the corresponding API domain.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Jotform modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Jotform Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nForms\n\nCreate a New Form\n\nNote: Refer to the Jotform API documentation for details regarding how to enter questions and emails.\n\nList Form Questions\n\nAdd Questions to Form\n\nForm Submissions\n\nWatch for Submissions\n\nGet Form Submissions\n\nNote: The Order by field will sort submissions by the selected field in descending order.\n\nGet User Submissions\n\nNote: The Order by field will sort submissions by the selected field in descending order.\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nGet Monthly User Usage\n\nNote: Refer to the Jotform API documentation for information regarding what user data is returned.\n\nJotform Troubleshooting\nUnable to Create a Webhook\n\nIf your connection is working but you are unable to create a webhook, your Jotform API Key may not have the necessary Full Access. To update the access level, go to your Jotform account profile settings, click on the API tab in the left sidebar, and ensure that your API Key has Full Access. If it has Read Access, click within the Permissions box and select Full Access.\n\nForms Are Not Displayed in Make\n\nIf your Jotform form is not visible in Make, first ensure that it has not been disabled in your Jotform account. In your Jotform account, open the form that is not visible in Make, click on More in the top menu, and ensure that the Disable option is not selected. If it is disabled, click on Enable to make your form visible.\n\nIf your form was already enabled or the form still is not visible after enabling, you can create a new connection in Make using a new Jotform API Key. Follow the instructions in the Connect Jotform to Make section to create a new API Key and establish the connection.\n\nJotform\nConnect Jotform to Make\nBuild Jotform Scenarios\nJotform Troubleshooting\nUnable to Create a Webhook\nForms Are Not Displayed in Make\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\n123FormBuilder\nAidaForm\nBasin\nCognito Forms\nContact Form 7\nFastField\nFormCrafts\nFormidable Forms\nFormsite\nGoogle Forms\nGravity Forms\nInMoment\nJotform\nPaperform\nPointerpro\nPoptin\nQuestionPro\nRefiner\nResponseSuite\nSoundCloud\nSurvey123\nSurveybot\nSurveyMonkey\nSurveySparrow\nTally\nTypebot\nTypeform\nVideoAsk\nWufoo\nZoho Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsSurveys and FormsSurveyMonkey\nSurveyMonkey\n\nWith SurveyMonkey modules in Make, you can create, retrieve, and search for collectors, retrieve and search for surveys and responses, retrieve your info, and watch new response events in your SurveyMonkey account.\n\nTo get started with SurveyMonkey, create an account at surveymonkey.com.\n\nNote\n\nRefer to the SurveyMonkey API documentation for the list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect SurveyMonkey to Make\n\nLog in to your Make account and add a SurveyMonkey module to a scenario.\n\nClick Add next to the Connection field.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, you will first be prompted to add a Webhook. Click Add next to the Webhook field, followed by Add next to the Connection field.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom application's Client ID and Client Secret values. To create these values, see the Create App ID and Secret for SurveyMonkey section.\n\nClick Save.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more SurveyMonkey modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nCreate App ID and Secret for SurveyMonkey\n\nYou can create your own application and connect it to Make using the App ID and Secret values from the application. To create these credentials:\n\nGo to your SurveyMonkey Developer My Apps page.\n\nClick Add a New App.\n\nFill in the App Nickname and App Creator fields, select the App Type, and click Create App.\n\nClick on the Settings tab, update the OAuth Redirect URL to https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/survey-monkey, and click Submit Changes.\n\nScroll down to the Scopes section, update your required scopes, and click Update Scopes.\n\nNote: If you update the app's scopes after creating the connection, you will be prompted in Make to update the connection by clicking Continue when adding a new module.\n\nScroll back up the page to the Credentials section, copy your Client ID and Secret, and store them in a safe place.\n\nYou will use these credentials in the Client ID and Client Secret fields when establishing the connection in Make.\n\nBuild SurveyMonkey Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nCreate a Collector\n\nCreates a new collector.\n\nGet a Collector\n\nRetrieves a collector's information.\n\nSearch for a Collector\n\nRetrieves a list of collectors.\n\nGet a Survey\n\nRetrieves a specific survey's information.\n\nSearch for a Survey\n\nReturns a list of surveys.\n\nGet a Response\n\nRetrieves response information with a given ID.\n\nNote: A paid SurveyMonkey account is required (Advantage or higher).\n\nSearch for a Response\n\nReturns a list of responses.\n\nNew Response Event\n\nTriggers when a new response event occurs.\n\nGet My Info\n\nReturns the current user's account details including their plan.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nNote\n\nModule Survey fields list surveys by title, unless otherwise stated.\n\nSurveyMonkey\nConnect SurveyMonkey to Make\nCreate App ID and Secret for SurveyMonkey\nBuild SurveyMonkey Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\n123FormBuilder\nAidaForm\nBasin\nCognito Forms\nContact Form 7\nFastField\nFormCrafts\nFormidable Forms\nFormsite\nGoogle Forms\nGravity Forms\nInMoment\nJotform\nPaperform\nPointerpro\nPoptin\nQuestionPro\nRefiner\nResponseSuite\nSoundCloud\nSurvey123\nSurveybot\nSurveyMonkey\nSurveySparrow\nTally\nTypebot\nTypeform\nVideoAsk\nWufoo\nZoho Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsSurveys and FormsGoogle Forms\nGoogle Forms \n\nWith Google Forms modules in Make, you can search, create, retrieve, and update forms and move forms to trash, watch, list, and retrieve responses, and watch, search, add, update, and delete responses in Google Forms.\n\nTo use the Google Forms modules, you must have a Google account. You can create an account at docs.google.com/forms/.\n\nTo upgrade to a new version of the Google Forms app, you need to upgrade all modules manually by Replacing Legacy Modules with New Modules.\n\nRefer to the Google Forms API Documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nNote\n\nMake's use and transfer of information received from Google APIs to any other app will adhere to Google API Services User Data Policy.\n\nConnect Google Forms to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Google Forms module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Switch on the Show advanced settings toggle and enter your Google Cloud Console project client credentials. For more information, see the Create and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Forms section below.\n\nClick the Sign in with Google.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Google Form modules. If your connection needs reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Forms\nBuild Google Forms Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nForm\n\nSearch Forms\n\nCreate a Form\n\nGet a Form\n\nUpdate a Form\n\nNote: For Item Changes, Location refers to the item's position on the list of all form items. The very first item is 0, the second item is 1, and so on. To add an item at the very beginning of your form, use 0 as the location.\n\nMove a Form to Trash\n\nResponse\n\nWatch Responses\n\nList Responses\n\nGet a Response\n\nLegacy\n\nWatch Responses in Google Sheets\n\nValue render option\n\n\t\n\nFormatted value: Values will be calculated and formatted in the reply according to the cell's formatting. Formatting is based on the spreadsheet's locale, not the requesting user's locale. For example, if A1 is 1.23 and A2 is =A1 and formatted as currency, then A2 will return $1.23.\n\nUnformatted value: Values will be calculated, but not formatted in the reply. For example, if A1 is 1.23 and A2 is =A1 and formatted as currency, then A2 will return 1.23.\n\nFormula: Values will not be calculated. For example, if A1 is 1.23 and A2 is =A1 and formatted as currency, then A2 will return =A1.\n\n\n\n\nDate and time render option\n\n\t\n\nSpecifies how dates, times, and duration should be represented in the output. This is ignored if Value render option (above) is set to Formatted value.\n\nSearch Responses in Google Sheets\n\nValue render option\n\n\t\n\nFormatted value: Values will be calculated and formatted in the reply according to the cell's formatting. Formatting is based on the spreadsheet's locale, not the requesting user's locale. For example, if A1 is 1.23 and A2 is =A1 and formatted as currency, then A2 will return $1.23.\n\nUnformatted value: Values will be calculated, but not formatted in the reply. For example, if A1 is 1.23 and A2 is =A1 and formatted as currency, then A2 will return 1.23.\n\nFormula: Values will not be calculated. For example, if A1 is 1.23 and A2 is =A1 and formatted as currency, then A2 will return =A1.\n\n\n\n\nDate and time render option\n\n\t\n\nSpecifies how dates, times, and duration should be represented in the output. This is ignored if Value render option (above) is set to Formatted value.\n\nSearch Responses in Google Sheets (advanced)\n\nNote: For the Filter field, define the search query using the Google Charts Query Language.\n\nE.g. select * where C = \"John\" to retrieve all values for the row where the C column is \"John\".\n\nAdd a Response in Google Sheets\n\nNote: For the Timestamp column, use the following value: formatDate(now;DD/MM/YYYY HH:mm;UTC)\n\nUpdate a Response in Google Sheets\n\nNote: For the Value input option field, Raw will not parse the values entered by the user and are stored as-is. User entered will parse the value as if the user typed them into the UI. Numbers will remain numbers, but strings may be converted to numbers, dates, etc., following the same rules that are applied when entering text into a cell via the Google Sheets UI.\n\nDelete a Response in Google Sheets\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nGoogle Forms\nConnect Google Forms to Make\nCreate and configure a Google Cloud Console project for Google Forms\nBuild Google Forms Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

To get access to a developer account, raise a request with the FastField support team within your FastField user account. You will receive your FastField developer account login details via email.\n\nRefer to the FastField API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect FastField to Make\n\nTo connect your FastField account to Make, you must obtain an API Key from your FastField developer account.\n\nLog in to your FastField developer account.\n\nIn the top right corner, click on your Name > Profile.\n\nIn the Your subscriptions section, click Show next to either your Primary key or Secondary key.\n\nCopy the key value. You will use this value to connect to Make.\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a FastField module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Username and Password fields, enter your Fastfield user account credentials. Do not enter your Fastfield developer account credentials.\n\nIn the API Key field, paste the key value copied in Step 4.\n\nClick Save.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more FastField modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet Up FastField Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nFastField Portal Views\n\nTo set up Fastfield webhooks, ensure that your FastField user portal is set to the New Portal view, not the Classic Portal view. To determine which portal view you are using, click on your profile icon in the bottom of the left sidebar.\n\nIf you see the Try Our New Portal option, click on it to go to the New Portal view and configure the webhook as described below.\n\nIf you see the Return To Classic Portal option, you are already in the New Portal and can configure the webhook as described below.\n\nOnce you have finished configuring the webhook, you can return to your preferred portal view by once again clicking on your profile icon in the bottom of the left sidebar and selecting the portal option.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd a FastField instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nLog in to your FastField user account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click on Account > Company Settings.\n\nNote: If you do not see the Account option in the left sidebar, refer to the FastField Portal Views information above.\n\nIn the top menu, click on Data Delivery.\n\nIn the Webhook section, paste the address copied in step 4 into the Form Submit URL field.\n\nClick Save.\n\nFastField will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild FastField Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nDispatch\n\nList Dispatches by a User\n\nCreate a Dispatch\n\nGlobal Lists\n\nNote: When entering a File Name, include the file extension.     "title": "Zapier",
    "url": "https://www.make.com/en/help/apps/process-management/zapier#content-wrapper",
    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nApuTime\nAX Semantics\nBeLazy\nCaflou\nEasyship\nIFTTT\nMake\nMetatask\nSeliom\nSimplero\nTallyfy\nTookan\nZapier\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsProcess ManagementZapier\nZapier\nGetting started with Zapier\n\nWe built the Zapier modules to give you even more flexibility with your automations by letting you exchange data between a scenario on Make and a zap on Zapier.\n\nCurrently, the following modules are available:\n\nTrigger: Receive Data (from a Zap)\n\nAction: Send Data (to a Zap)\n\nReceive data\n\nFollow the steps below to receive data from a Zap in a Scenario using the Receive Data module:\n\nStep 1: Setup a new Zap or go to an existing one that contains the modules from which you wish to send data to Make.\n\nClick on 'Add a Step' to insert the action Webhooks\n\nChoose POST as the method under the Webhooks by Zapier and click 'Continue'\n\nStep 2: Create a new scenario on Make using the Zapier - Receive data as the first module in your scenario.\n\nClick the 'Add' button to create a new webhook\n\nName your webhook and click Save\n\nCopy the newly generated webhook URL and let the webhook wait to receive sample data\n\nStep 3: Go back to Zapier and fill in the following values in the setup fields of the Webhooks by Zapier - POST action:\n\nURL: Enter the webhook URL obtained from the Make scenario in the previous step\n\nPayload Type: Json\n\nData: Specify the data you want to send to Make (as Key, Value pairs)\n\nContinue to the next step and click 'Send Test to Webhooks by Zapier'. This will send sample data to the Make webhook which had been listening for data\n\nOnce the webhook receives the sample data, click 'OK' to continue to the next module to build your scenario\n\nOnce your scenario setup is complete, make sure you save it and turn it on to experience the magic!\n\nSend data\n\nTo send data from an Make Scenario to a Zap using the Send data module, follow the steps below:\n\nStep 1: Create a new Zap in Zapier and select Webhooks by Zapier - Catch Hook as the first module in your Zap and click 'Save + Continue'\n\nIn the next step, simply click 'Continue'\n\nCopy the generated webhook URL into your clipboard. You will need it in the next step\n\nStep 2: Go to Make and insert the module Zapier - Send data to your scenario that shall send data to Zapier\n\nPaste the Webhook URL obtained in last step and specify the data that shall be sent to Zapier as key, value pairs (Simple) or JSON (Advanced)\n\nGo back to the Zap and click 'Ok, I did this'. Zapier is now waiting to receive data from Make.\n\nStep 3: Go to the Make scenario and run it manually by clicking the 'Run once' button. This will send sample data to Zapier.\n\nZapier should confirm the receipt of the data and finish the configuration of the webhook.\n\nOnce the connection between Make and Zapier is established, you can add other actions to your zap and achieve your intended integration.\n\nHappy Automating!\n\nZapier\nGetting started with Zapier\nReceive data\nSend data\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

If you do not have one, you can create a Simplero account at simplero.com/accounts/new.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnect Simplero to Make\n\nTo connect your Simplero account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Simplero account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\nLogin to your Simplero account.\n\nClick Settings > Integrations > Create New API Key.\n\nClick the copy () against the API key to copy the API key to your clipboard.\n\nGo to Make and open the Simplero module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied in step 3.\n\nIn the Application field, enter your application name. If your account's URL address is www.xyz.simplero.com then your application is xyz.\n\nIn the Email field, enter the email address used for creating the Simplero account, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nPurchases\nWatch Purchase Added\nWatch Purchase Deleted\nCreate a Purchase\nTags\nWatch Tag Added\nWatch Tag Removed\nAdd a Tag to the Contact\nRemove a Tag from the Contact\nContacts\nGet a Contact\nCreate a Contact\nUpdate a Contact\nSubscription Lists\nWatch Subscription Added\nWatch Subscription Deleted\nList Subscriber Lists\nSubscribe to a List\nUnsubscribe from a List\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Products\nConnecting to Simplero Webhook using Make\n\nOpen any Watch module, establish the connection as mentioned in the respective modules, click Save, copy the URL address to your clipboard, click OK, and save the trigger.\n\nLogin to your Simplero account. Click Settings > Triggers > Add trigger.\n\nFor this object type\n\n\t\n\nSelect the object type for which you want to add the trigger. For example, product, list.After you select the object type, choose the specific object for which you want to add the trigger.\n\n\n\n\nWhen this happens\n\n\t\n\nSelect the option for which action you want to add the trigger. For example, Purchase: activated.\n\n\n\n\nValue\n\n\t\n\nEnter the value if applicable.\n\n\n\n\nDo this\n\n\t\n\nSelect the action to perform when the specified action happens. For example, send an email.Once you select the action, a field auto-populates to select (enter) the particular action details. For example, enter the email address to send the email.\n\n\n\n\nWhich email\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email address to notify.\n\n\n\n\nCondition\n\n\t\n\nSelect the condition for which you want to receive the trigger.\n\n\n\n\nOnly fire once per contact\n\n\t\n\nSelect the checkbox to receive only one trigger for one single contact.\n\n\n\n\nEnable this trigger\n\n\t\n\nSelect the checkbox to enable the webhook.\n\nClick Save to add the webhook.\n\nSimplero\nGetting Started with Simplero\nConnect Simplero to Make\nPurchases\nWatch Purchase Added\nWatch Purchase Deleted\nCreate a Purchase\nTags\nWatch Tag Added\nWatch Tag Removed\nAdd a Tag to the Contact\nRemove a Tag from the Contact\nContacts\nGet a Contact\nCreate a Contact\nUpdate a Contact\nSubscription Lists\nWatch Subscription Added\nWatch Subscription Deleted\nList Subscriber Lists\nSubscribe to a List\nUnsubscribe from a List\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get Products\nConnecting to Simplero Webhook using Make\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

    "title": "IFTTT",
    "url": "https://www.make.com/en/help/apps/process-management/ifttt#content-wrapper",
    "html": "Skip to main content\nMake Help Center\nRelease notes\nGeneral\nAI in Make\nAccess management\nConnections\nScenarios\nTutorials\nModules\nMapping\nTools\nFunctions\nErrors\nDevices\nApps\nIntroduction to Make apps\nAI\nBuilt-in apps\nBusiness Intelligence\nBusiness Operations and ERPs\nCommerce\nCommunication\nCRM and Sales tools\nCustomer Support\nDatabase\nEducation\nFile and Document Management\nHR management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nApuTime\nAX Semantics\nBeLazy\nCaflou\nEasyship\nIFTTT\nMake\nMetatask\nSeliom\nSimplero\nTallyfy\nTookan\nZapier\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsProcess ManagementIFTTT\nIFTTT\nGetting started with IFTTT\n\nWe built the IFTTT modules to give you even more flexibility with your automations by letting you exchange data between a scenario on Make and an applet on IFTTT.\n\nCurrently, the following modules are available:\n\nTrigger: Receive data from an applet\n\nAction: Send data to an applet\n\nThe above modules also allow you to connect and control arbitrary IoT devices connected to IFTTT.\n\n----\n\nReceive data\n\nUsing the Receive data module, you can get data from an arbitrary trigger in the IFTTT applet. Follow the steps below to achieve this:\n\nCreate a new applet on IFTTT or go to an existing one that contains the trigger from which you'd like to send data to Make\n\nInsert the action Webhook - Make a web request. The applet should look like: If Your trigger then Webhook - Make a web request\n\nCreate a new scenario on Make using IFTTT - Receive data as the first module\n\nClick the 'Add' button to create a new webhook\n\nName your webhook and click Save\n\nCopy the newly generated webhook URL and let the webhook wait to receive sample data\n\nGo to IFTTT and in the settings of the Webhook - Make a web request action fill in the following values:\n\nURL: Paste the webhook URL obtained from Make in the previous step\n\nMethod: POST\n\nContent Type: application/json\n\nBody: JSON with data you want to send to Make\n\nExample JSON:\n\n               {\n\"Value1Label\": \"{{Value1}}\",\n\"Value2Label\": \"{{Value2}}\"\n}\n            \n\nThe JSON can contain an arbitrary amount of values. Value1Label is a label how the value will be presented in Make. {{Value1}} is an ingredient from the IFTTT trigger.\n\nTurn your IFTTT applet on and run it once. This will send sample data to the Make webhook which had been listening for data\n\nOnce the webhook receives the sample data, click 'OK' to continue and use the data received from IFTTT in subsequent modules of your Make scenario.\n\nComplete your scenario in Make and turn it on.\n\n----\n\nSend data\n\nFollow the steps below to send data from Make to a trigger in an IFTTT applet and run any IFTTT action using the Send data module:\n\nCreate a new applet on the IFTTT Platform (https://platform.ifttt.com/)\n\nUse Webhooks - Receive a web request as the trigger for your applet\n\nScroll below to enter an event name which you will need to enter when setting up the module on Make\n\nInsert the action you want to control from Make. The applet should look like: If Webhooks - Receive a web request then Your action\n\nActivate your applet.\n\nGo to Make and insert the module IFTTT - Send data to your scenario that shall send data to IFTTT\n\nGo to https://ifttt.com/maker_webhooks, click 'Documentation' on the upper-right corner and copy your key from the documentation page\n\nClick 'Add' next to the Connectiondrop-down to create a new connection between Make and IFTTT. You will be requested to fill in the key obtained in the last step\n\nEnter the event name that you had entered when creating the applet on IFTTT\n\nLastly, map the data in the fields Value1, Value2, and Value3. These values will be sent to IFTTT\n\nOnce your scenario setup on Make is complete, make sure you save it and turn it on to begin sending data to your newly created IFTTT applet. Now you can use this data in subsequent actions in your applet to achieve the intended integration!\n\nIFTTT\nGetting started with IFTTT\nReceive data\nSend data\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

For example: /whoami\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Seliom API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET\n\nto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST\n\nto create a new entry.\n\nPUT\n\nto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH\n\nto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE\n\nto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - Get User\n\nThe following API call returns the current user details from your Seliom account:\n\nURL:\n\n/whoami\n\nMethod:\n\nGET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body.\n\nIn our example, current user details were returned:\n\nSeliom\nGetting Started with Seliom\nConnecting Seliom to Make\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get User\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

your Make account, add a YouCanBook.me module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nEnter your YouCanBook.me Email Address.\n\nIn the Password field, enter one of the following:\n\nYour YouCanBook.me account password\n\nThe API key for your account (see the YouCanBook.me Accessing your account API key documentation)\n\nA one time token received via email\n\nA session token with a limited life span\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more YouCanBook.me modules. If you do not have one, you can create a BeLazy account at belazy.cat.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting BeLazy to Make\n\nTo connect your BeLazy account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your BeLazy account.\n\nLog in to your BeLazy account.\n\nClick on your profile icon in the top-right corner and select the Api access tokens option from the drop-down menu.\n\nClick the GENERATE TOKEN button.\n\nCopy the provided access token.\n\nGo to Make and open the BeLazy module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nEnter the API Key you have copied in step 4 to the respective field and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nAllows you to perform a custom API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your BeLazy account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.belazy.cat/api. E.g. /projects/v1\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the BeLazy API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET\n\nto retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST\n\nto create a new entry.\n\nPUT\n\nto update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH\n\nto make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE\n\nto delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Connections\n\nThe following API call returns all connections from your BeLazy account:\n\nURL:\n\n/connections/v1/vendor\n\nMethod:\n\nGET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body.\n\nIn our example, 2 connections were returned:\n\nBeLazy\nGetting Started with BeLazy\nConnecting BeLazy to Make\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Connections\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsProductivityXero Projects\nXero Projects\n\nWith Xero Projects modules in Make, you can create, update, delete, list, and retrieve tasks, projects, and time entries, update project statuses and details, and retrieve project users from your Xero Projects account.\n\nTo get started with Xero Projects, create an account at xero.com. Xero Projects is included in the Xero Established Plan at no charge per user. If you do not have the Established Plan, visit the Manage your Xero Projects subscription page for more information regarding adding Xero Projects to your account.\n\nNote\n\nRefer to the Xero Projects API documentation for the list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Xero Projects to Make\n\nTo connect your Xero Projects account to Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account and add a Xero Projects module to a scenario.\n\nClick Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and choose the Scopes for the connection. Choose only the minimum scopes required for your intended use. Each module's required scopes can be found in the Build Xero Projects Scenarios section below. For additional information regarding scopes, refer to the Xero API documentation.\n\nGrant access to Make in the popup window. You may be prompted to sign in to your Xero Projects account first.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Xero Projects modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nNote\n\nIf you receive an error while creating the connection, you must manually add the scopes. Go to step 4 follow the instructions to do so.\n\nWhen adding a new Xero Projects module to a scenario using an existing connection, you may be prompted to update the connection permissions. Click Continue and Allow access to extend the permissions.\n\nBuild Xero Projects Scenarios\nTasks\n\nList Tasks\n\nScopes: projects\n\nGet a Task\n\nScopes: projects\n\nCreate a Task\n\nScopes: projects\n\nUpdate a Task\n\nScopes: projects\n\nDelete a Task\n\nNote: If the task has a service associated or status invoiced it will not be removed.\n\nScopes: projects\n\nProjects\n\nList Project Users\n\nScopes: projects\n\nList Projects\n\nScopes: projects accounting.contacts.read\n\nGet a Project\n\nScopes: projects\n\nCreate a Project\n\nScopes: projects accounting.contacts.read\n\nUpdate a Project Status\n\nScopes: projects\n\nUpdate Project Details\n\nScopes: projects\n\nTime Entries\n\nList Time Entries\n\nScopes: projects\n\nGet a Time Entry\n\nScopes: projects\n\nCreate a Time Entry\n\nScopes: projects\n\nUpdate a Time Entry\n\nScopes: projects\n\nDelete a Time Entry\n\nNote: If the time entry has the status invoiced it will not be removed.\n\nScopes: projects\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nScopes: accounting.settings accounting.settings.read\n\nXero Projects\nConnect Xero Projects to Make\nBuild Xero Projects Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsProductivityWorkstack\nWorkstack\n\nThe Workstack modules allow you to watch, create, update, retrieve, and delete projects, todo lists, tasks, and meetings in your Workstack account.\n\nGetting Started with Workstack\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Workstack account\n\nIn order to use Workstack with Make, it is necessary to have a Workstack account. If you do not have one, you can create a Workstack account at app.workstack.io/register.\n\nConnecting Workstack to Make\n\nTo connect your Workstack account to Make you need to obtain the Token from your Workstack account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\n1. Log in to your Workstack account.\n\n2. Click Your Profile Icon > Link to Other Apps. Enter a name for the token and click Create.\n\n3. Copy the API Key to your clipboard and save it for future use.\n\n4. Go toMake and open the Workstack module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n5. In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\n6. In the API Token field, enter the API key copied in step 3 and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nProject\nWatch Created Projects\n\nTriggers when a new project is created.\n\nCaution\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the Workstack as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Workstack account.\n\nWatch Projects\n\nTriggers when a new project is created.\n\nNote\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the Workstack as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\nCreate a Project\n\nCreates a new project.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nProject Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the project.\n\n\n\n\nNote\n\n\t\n\nEnter the details about the project.\n\n\n\n\nColor Code\n\n\t\n\nEnter the appropriate color code for the project in the /^#[a-fA-F0-9]+$/format. Must have the size of 7. For example, #f82937\n\n\n\n\nTime in Minutes\n\n\t\n\nEnter the time allocated for the project in minutes.\n\n\n\n\nStart Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the project starts.\n\n\n\n\nEnd Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the project ends.\n\n\n\n\nCompleted\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the project is completed:\n\nYes\n\nNo\n\nNot defined\n\n\n\n\nCompleted at\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the project is completed.\n\n\n\n\nPosition\n\n\t\n\nEnter the position of the project on the priority list. The value must be higher than or equal to 0.\n\n\n\n\nUsers\n\n\t\n\nAdd the users who are assigned for the project.\n\nGet a Project\n\nRetrieves an existing project by ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nProject ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Project ID whose details you want to retrieve.\n\nUpdate a Project\n\nUpdates an existing project by ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nProject ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Project ID whose details you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nProject Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the project.\n\n\n\n\nNote\n\n\t\n\nEnter the details about the project.\n\n\n\n\nColor Code\n\n\t\n\nEnter the appropriate color code for the project in the /^#[a-fA-F0-9]+$/format. Must have the size of 7. For example, #f82937\n\n\n\n\nTime in Minutes\n\n\t\n\nEnter the time allocated for the project in minutes.\n\n\n\n\nStart Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the project starts.\n\n\n\n\nEnd Date\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the project ends.\n\n\n\n\nCompleted\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the project is completed:\n\nYes\n\nNo\n\nNot defined\n\n\n\n\nCompleted at\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the project is completed.\n\n\n\n\nPosition\n\n\t\n\nEnter the position of the project on the priority list. The value must be higher than or equal to 0.\n\n\n\n\nUsers\n\n\t\n\nAdd the users who are assigned for the project.\n\nDelete a Project\n\nDeletes an existing project by ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nProject ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Project ID you want to delete.\n\nList Projects\n\nLists all projects.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of projects Make should return during one scenario execution cycle.\n\nTodo Lists\nWatch Created Todo Lists\n\nTriggers when a new todo list is created.\n\nNote\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the Workstack as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\nCreate a Todo List\n\nCreates a new todo list.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nProject ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Project ID whose todo list you want to create.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the todo list.\n\n\n\n\nNote\n\n\t\n\nEnter the details about the todo list.\n\n\n\n\nMinutes\n\n\t\n\nEnter the time allocated for the todo list in minutes.\n\n\n\n\nStart\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the todo list starts.\n\n\n\n\nEnd\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the todo list ends.\n\n\n\n\nCompleted\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the todo list is completed:\n\nYes\n\nNo\n\nNot defined\n\n\n\n\nCompleted at\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the todo list is completed.\n\n\n\n\nPosition\n\n\t\n\nEnter the position of the todo list on the priority list. The value must be higher than or equal to 0.\n\nGet a Todo List\n\nRetrieves a todo by ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nTodo List ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Project ID whose to-do list whose details you want to retrieve.\n\nUpdate a Todo List\n\nUpdates an existing task by ID.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nTodo List ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Todo List ID whose details you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nProject ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Project ID whose todo list you want to create.\n\n\n\n\nName\n\n\t\n\nEnter a name for the todo list.\n\n\n\n\nNote\n\n\t\n\nEnter the details about the todo list.\n\n\n\n\nMinutes\n\n\t\n\nEnter the time allocated for the todo list in minutes.\n\n\n\n\nStart\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the todo list starts.\n\n\n\n\nEnd\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the todo list ends.\n\n\n\n\nCompleted\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether the todo list is completed:\n\nYes\n\nNo\n\nNot defined\n\n\n\n\nCompleted at\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date when the todo list is completed.\n\n\n\n\nPosition\n\n\t\n\nEnter the position of the todo list on the priority list. For example: /users\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Workstack API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET to retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST to create a new entry.\n\nPUT to update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH to make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE to delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Projects\n\nThe following API call returns all the projects from your Workstack account:\n\nURL:/projects\n\nMethod:GET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > data. In our example, 3 projects were returned:\n\nWorkstack\nGetting Started with Workstack\nConnecting Workstack to Make\nProject\nWatch Created Projects\nWatch Projects\nCreate a Project\nGet a Project\nUpdate a Project\nDelete a Project\nList Projects\nTodo Lists\nWatch Created Todo Lists\nCreate a Todo List\nGet a Todo List\nUpdate a Todo List\nDelete a Todo List\nList All Todo Without a Project\nTask\nWatch Created Tasks\nCreated a Task\nGet a Task\nUpdate a Task\nDelete a Task\nList Task for a User\nMeeting\nWatch Created Meetings\nWatch Meetings\nCreate a Meeting\nGet a Meeting\nUpdate a Meeting\nDelete a Meeting\nList Meeting\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Projects\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."
